Unlike green/white papers, blue papers were issued by the central NBTHK authority in Tokyo, not the provincial branches where authentication scandals occurred. More reliable than other Kicho-era papers but still not up to modern Hozon standards in rigor. See: koshu-tokubetsu-kicho." [ref=e316]':

A sayagaki typically includes the smith attribution, blade characteristics, measurements, and date of examination." [ref=e6947]:
